<date>1495062006571</date><rate>5< /rate>< Text>
I studied at the Meisner Technique Studio for 2yrs, and graduated in April 2016. OMG. I wish had had found out about this school when I first started acting. I moved to the bay area in 2013, after spending the last 6 years performing professionally in plays, sketch-comedy, and improv in Chicago. Being in a new city, I decided to take some time for myself and get back to training, and I feel so lucky to have found the this studio.

Jim and Melissa took my acting to levels I couldn't have imagined possible. I've never felt more free, connected, working moment-to-moment with my scene partners, than I did working and growing at this studio. I took acting classes, improv classes, you name it all over Chicago, and nothing was as thorough or step-by-step (brick-by-brick as Jim would say!) as the training they presented over the course of 2 years. They also gave me tons of new tools to build earned characters with depth, and ways of accessing and growing my imagination to serve the imaginary circumstances of a script.

There are tons of schools our there claiming to teach "meisner" technique (I studied at three such studios in Chicago where I grew, but felt like I was only scratching the surface of what we were doing) but none of did justice to the full-two year professional training as Sanford Meisner taught and intended it.  I feel really lucky that Jim continues Sandy's legacy by presenting this training class-by-class as it was taught to him.

If you're committed to your acting career, and want to grow as a person and an artist, do yourself a favor and interview at this school! :)</Text>

<Text>If you are a passionate actor, committed to the craft and with a strong desire to grow, then this is the school for you. This 2-year course teaches the Meisner technique in its purest form, following the same framework put in place by Sanford Meisner with building blocks and new tools introduced throughout the program. Scene work is a great opportunity to get to work with other acting partners and gain experience with live theater. You will practice many effective techniques that will get you in touch with your inner self, unchain your imagination and help you in the journey to become truthfully the character yourself. This class will give you a lot of freedom to express yourself on stage and follow your gut, it will help you be present, listen and react to your acting partner, overcome fears and be comfortable with public solitude.

Jim Jarrett and Melissa Thompson Esaia are very passionate and experienced coaches, they have worked with hundreds of actors over the years, they are extremely dedicated to the craft of acting, and very sensitive human beings. They take this class very seriously and truly care about your growth as an actor, sacrificing much of their time, and they expect the same level of commitment from you. They make the class a safe environment to express yourself freely and have fun playing. They offer honest and insightful feedback to your work that will help you grow as an actor. By the end of the program you will have all the tools for you to look back at your own work as you advance in your career and be able to tell what went well and what needs to be advanced. If you have the time, commitment and passion to dedicate to this journey, you will experience incredible growth as an actor and build resilience as a human being.

As a bonus point, you will become part of an large artistic family of talented actors, directors, writers and producers (all students or alumni from the same school) who collaborate on projects of live theater and films for the numerous showcases and festivals hosted by the school or outside.< /Text><Pics>None</Pics><response>None</response><Gmap_id>0x808586d7fd6fa127:0x49b19ba3cd6734f5< /Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

< review>
You don't need prior experience and you don't have to be certain that acting is right for you. Maybe you just have this nagging feeling that won't go away, a creative spark in you that refuses to be ignored. This is a safe place to uncover, explore, and expand what your creativity and imagination are capable of. This program is a commitment, but it takes time and dedication to peel the onion that is YOU.

So now that I've graduated, do I know for sure that acting is my calling in life? No, but within two months of completing the business class, I've booked 3 speaking roles; 2 TV pilots (one for NBC) and an independent film. Lucky? Yes, partially. But I pursued this on my own for 5+ years when I was younger and more "marketable," and never booked this much.

Are you hoping to experience just one or two creative breakthroughs? Or do you want to methodically learn and practice how to achieve them consistently? At this school, you will sharpen your instincts, become more brave, confident, and free. And who knows, you might decide to do a couple of acting gigs afterwards.< /review>

When I say that this training changed my life, I am not exaggerating in the slightest. I went into this training expecting to learn how to act, but I left it transformed as both and actor and a human being. I found a family that I will have in my life forever, I have no doubt about it.

I learned the power of truthful acting (of which the only drawback is that now I can‚Äôt watch a badly acted movie or show without cringing), and I embraced emotions that I‚Äôd never allowed myself to feel, let alone express in any way. I improved my work ethic, empathy, and fueled a passion that I‚Äôd only ever dreamed of pursuing.

Growing up, I‚Äôd always wanted to perform in some way, being a musical and creative person. But my shyness and stage fright made that nearly impossible. By the time I arrived at the Meisner Technique Studio, I‚Äôd overcome the majority of my shyness, but my stage fright was still very much present. By the end of the first class, my stage fright was practically decimated.

That‚Äôs not to say that everything comes that easily. Jim has done an incredible job to honor the format of his mentor, Sanford Meisner. In honoring that, he expects a lot from his students. He pushes us and makes us better, but in my experience it was ALWAYS for the best. There were times that feedback hurt, but you HAVE to take your ego out of the equation the second you enter the studio. This training is about turning you into a truthful actor, and everything that Jim does goes towards that goal.

After the formal training, Jim also offers an optional business class that teaches students how to enter the business world of acting. Everything from auditioning to landing an agent, and from building a resume to creating a pitch deck. I was lucky enough to take this class from both Jim and his incredible daughter, Kyla. She knows SO much about this industry, having worked on the other side of it for some time, and she is an amazing teacher.

If you‚Äôre interested in learning to be an actor, this is the place to go. It‚Äôll be tough, but every second is worth it.< /Text>

I come from a family of established folk and becoming an actor wasn't exciting news for anyone who knew me except for myself. Well it was a tough transition from high school going into acting school instead of a traditional college. However I can say with complete confidence that this was the best decision of my life thus far; choosing to study at The Meisner Technique Studio for two years to learn how to act. The term 'bildungsroman' often comes to mind when I reflect on my experience here. I was an 18 year old boy coming out of high school and being thrown into a whole new world filled with a diverse community of adults and being treated as one with zero exceptions as to my age. The result; an emotional development created over a course of two years that most people wait their whole lives to experience. That is not a bold statement nor is it come from a place of ego or pride--it is simply a fact of the capability of the genius technique created by Sanford Meisner and perfectly preserved and passed down by my two teachers during my time, Jim and Melissa.

If you read other reviews on this list you'll notice the term "life changing" being used frequent and often. My point exactly, lucky for me I found this place in my youth. My suggestion to you--if you are an actor and ready to be an actor for your life's sake--then get to work and get yourself an interview with Jim Jarrett. Here at The Meisner Technique Studio you will be pushed to discover yourself and pushed to give your full and complete attention to what this is, your dream of being an actor. When and if you finish this training, you are an actor. Ultimately I must warn you this training, just as everything in your life, is on you. Your teacher is there to guide you and teach you, your peers are there to support you along side their own journeys and vice versa but your time here can only be as great as you make it. <time>1495519550279< /time><rate>5</rate>< review>
If you are seriously interested in studying acting or becoming an actor, this is an excellent school.  Jim and Melissa care deeply about the craft of acting and about their students and alumni.

Before you request an interview, it‚Äôs important to realize that Jim and Melissa take acting and their School very seriously, they are very committed to their jobs and they expect commitment from their students.  This is not a class to undertake casually.  Students who don‚Äôt show the requisite commitment either leave voluntarily, or are expelled.  This sounds harsh, but it isn‚Äôt really:  There is a lot of emphasis on pair-work out of class, in order to practice what has been taught.  You want to be sure that if you are going to be dedicated, then your classmates are going to be dedicated also, so if everybody knows that you have to do the work, or get kicked out, it helps keep everybody honest.  If you are willing and able to put the work in, you have nothing to worry about it.

I suppose in a nutshell what the Meisner Technique teaches you is how to behave truthfully under imaginary circumstances.  Good actors are believable.  ‚ÄúWould somebody do/say that in real life?‚Äù  Truthful behavior is very much the standard to which students are held as actors.  The Technique gradually teaches you how to be truthful as an actor.  If you don‚Äôt value, or don‚Äôt think you might come to value, behaving truthfully under imaginary circumstances, then this School is not for you.

Observations
Acting experience is not necessary to be accepted in the school.
Over the two years, the people who put the most work in, tend to progress the most.
The bias of the School is towards meaningful, contemporary work i.e. serious stuff.
If your ambition is to be in Neil Simon plays and/or musicals, this School will give you the skills to be a present, truthful actor in those areas, but you may be happier studying elsewhere.  Similarly if you like skits and/or effecting behavior, rather than producing it from within, this School is probably not the best fit for you.  (This is not to say Neil Simon plays or skits don‚Äôt have value, but this is the Meisner Technique.)

Although the emphasis is on acting from within, rather than effecting, there is also a strong emphasis on being an emotionally healthy person, who respects themselves and others.

What you won‚Äôt get: voice training, Shakespeare, dance training, fight training.  It‚Äôs just the core.

The best way to approach the classes is to be completely open to the approach and to the feedback.

Personal growth: if you complete the training, you will grow as an actor and a person; you will see some amazing things from your classmates.
Jim Jarrett‚Äôs play ‚ÄúMeisner‚Äù is an excellent introduction to Sanford Meisner and his philosophy.

I have yet to meet a graduate of the Meisner Technique Studio who regretted the time they spent there.

Whatever you decide to do, I wish you the best of luck.<//review>

My work in acting before coming to this school was false, phony, and extremely acted. I had no idea what the hell I was doing, and on top of that I was constantly playing the character instead of simply being the character.

<rating>5</rating><Time>1483041159136<//Time>< Review>
If you have the courage and the tenacity to forge for yourself a clear vision for your life and career, the training and wisdom with which Jim Jarrett and Melissa Thompson Esaia can empower you is absolutely invaluable, not only as it relates to the most truthful and sensitive form of acting made possible through the incredible teachings of Sanford Meisner, but perhaps more importantly, as it relates to elevating the human spirit and becoming a better person in the end.

<review>A few years ago I looked in the mirror and asked myself "What are you waiting for? How long will you keep dreaming but be too scared to go after that dream?" Fast forward a few years and I am googling "The Meisner Technique" and "Meisner schools" from my computer in Vancouver, Canada, I came across a few schools in my area but they just didn't resonate with me.

Then I came across The Meisner Technique Studio in San Francisco. I clicked on the link and saw videos of Jim Jarrett teaching some of his classes. I was immediately drawn to what I was seeing. I had never met the man, but his passion, humility and warmth was more than apparent.
Everything he was expressing about the craft of acting immediately resonated with me. I thought "I really need to train with this person".

After being accepted into the training program I needed to try to figure out how I could move to San Francisco. Jim and Melissa went above and beyond in trying to help make my move as smooth as possible.
They connected with a former student who was Canadian who completed the training and she told me her experiences of traveling back and forth between The US and Canada during her 2 years of training.
They reached out to current and former students to try to help me find a place to live.
They are always available for a chat when things are going sideways for me and I need someone to talk to or if I am having trouble understanding a new exercise in class. I have been given so much support from the school and I haven't even talked about the training yet...lol.

If you are new to acting or want to take your craft to a whole new level of truth and authenticity, I highly recommend training at The Meisner Technique Studio. The training is intense and so worth it. It means a lot to me that the training is delivered EXACTLY as Sanford Meisner wanted it to be taught. It also means a lot to me that my teacher Jim Jarrett was not only taught by Sanford Meisner but he was also taught how to teach "The Meisner Technique" by Sanford Meisner. Somedays in class, I can feel Sanford Meisner in the room watching all of us students try to figure out these amazing teachings he created. I hope he is proud, sometimes I hope he gets a good laugh as I fumble my way through a new exercise.

I am in my last 6 moths of the 2 year program and I have never been as free as an actor or as a human being. I feel completely safe when I work with Jim and Melissa. I trust them and the process. I see how hard they work and how dedicated they are to the school and to each student. They really do want the best for everyone who trains with them.
I am inspired by them and my classmates on a daily basis.

Training with The Meisner Technique Studio is so much more than an acting class. I've been given a supportive community who understands what it means to have a dream and go after it. I can't tell you how precious that is, to have someone look at you and say "I believe in you and I believe in your dream...and I will do everything I can to help you." I get that on a daily basis from my teachers Jim Jarrett and Melissa Thompson Esaia.
So, what are you waiting for?
And please don't hesitate to reach out to me if you need clarification on anything I said or have any questions.

Cheers,

The Most LIFE CHANGING thing I've done as an adult! It feels like it has to be the best acting school in the world, and that feeling I get... could very well be right. The Meisner Technique Studio is a hidden gem of an acting school in the beautiful Presidio of San Francisco. I can say that because I have actually had the privilege to have studied under Jim Jarrett and Melissa Thompson Esaia. The training is two years and in those years not only do you learn about the craft of acting but you learn about to beauty of being a human, you learn about the beauty of you and I have learned to see the world through different lenses. Staying open and trusting the teachers is tremendously important because they are there to help you and they care.

I remember several years ago being at crossroads in life and was not sure about what to do. I had gone to many acting studios and even taken classes at the university level but they never taught me craft, honestly, they didn't know what it meant. So in 2012 I heard about the Meisner Technique Studio because i saw Jim perform his play, "Meisner" in Los Angeles. Blown away. For any dreamer out there that has been contemplating where to study to further their dream, I encourage you to look into the Meisner Technique Studio. Look at their website, talk to the teachers( they will actually reach out to you), and the graduates of the training. Not third party solicitors that have never even stepped foot in the studio. <pics>None< /pics><review>If you want to study the brilliant methodical technique devised by reknowned acting teacher Sanford Meisner, this is, in my opinion, is the best place in the country to do it. Meisner wanted actors to behave truthfully, spontaneously, creatively under imaginary circumstances. Robert Duvall, Susan Sarandon, Gregory Peck are just a few of the greats who benefited from his training.

Jim Jarrett, who studied intensively under Meisner, and fellow teacher Melissa Thompson Esaia are determined to deliver the training as closely as possible to the way Meisner himself taught it.   At the same time, they beautifully and sensitively address the emotional, spiritual and practical challenges faced by working actors.

This is a professional school that places professional demands on its students. Yes, you are expected to show up on time. Yes, you are expected to work hard.   Jim and Melissa insist on creating a work atmosphere filled with respect, appreciation, a positive attitude. They are dedicated, hard-working and amazingly accessible to their students.

Jim and Melissa are intelligent and insightful teachers.  They are honest and demanding but also nurturing. They deal sensitively with actors, realizing we all place tender, difficult human feelings on the line as we work.  My time at the Meisner Technique Studio has fostered great friendships, and great opportunities to practice the craft of acting with other serious actors and directors.

Long before I started this training I worked professionally in New York City and in regional repertory theaters.  I studied with Uta Hagen, and with teachers who came out of the Actors Studio, the Atlantic Theatre Company and Meisner training.  But the best, most comprehensive acting schooling I've experienced came from Jim and Melissa. If you want to inject truth and spontaneity into your acting work, this is the place to be.< /review></record>

<Review>Editing my review after coming back here a couple more times!

Unfortunately they don't take CRV cans or plastic and they pay you very little for the stuff you bring there, but in my opinion that's not why you go there!

Right next to where you drop off your recyclables there is a shop there with tons of cool stuff you won't find anywhere else!  If you're into electronics they have tons of computer parts!  Tom, one of the employees, regularly assembles PCs out of the parts he comes across.  For what you pay and what you get it can be an incredible bargain for someone on a tight budget!

I bought some Delta 120mm PC case fans for my computer there at $4 a pop, while online they're like $15-$20.  Also found a Cherry made in Germany mechanical keyboard with Cherry MX Brown switches!  While the other guys there are nice enough, Tom's the one who really knows his stuff.  Def worth checking out for some unique oddities you won't find anywhere else!  Not many recycling centers have a store where you can buy used/surplus PC and other goods like they do!< /Review><pics>None</pics><resp>None</resp><GmapID>0x80db7e329e05e3bd:0xf62f7533d85afbd9< /GmapID></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
Was very surprised to find a poke place here. Thought I would check the reviews and see what others thought. This place lived up to the majority of reviews. The service was very pleasant and attentive.

There is a great variety of proteins. Portions are good. The mixed greens option for a base is great. So many toppings to choose from. The extra .70$ for avocado is a good deal.

The gal who served me made sure that she had included all that I asked for. Handled my order with care. Asked good questions to find out what I liked and also to make suggestions on a sauce.

As for the fish... I found it to be fresh and flavorful. It was mixed very well with the sauce that she suggested. I went with the house sauce. It was tangy and a hint of spice. Complimented everything I had chosen in the bowl. I had the large bowl with Salmon x2, scallops, yellowtail, albacore.

Great experience.

Would definitely recommend to others!< /Review>

< review>
A South Gate hallmark just like Greenspans. At first entrance the murals make it feel authentic, that feeling like your back to Mexico. The soccer memorabilia is a nice added touch for any soccer fan, the owner has the last two world cup balls and multiple jerseys on display. The food is great, good price and they don't skimp on the portions. I personally go for the torta, but they are also known for their huaraches. Overall a South Gate must have.< /review>
